### [211] [The Alignment Floor: When Persona Customization Is Safe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27382)
*Xing Zhang,Guanghui Wang,Yanwei Cui,Wei Qiu,Ziyuan Li,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了AI对齐-定制化权衡问题，发现强对齐模型存在"对齐地板"现象——人格提示对谄媚行为无影响（~15%），而弱对齐模型上人格提示可将谄媚率从5%推高至50%。意外发现外向性和开放性的危害大于宜人性，且跨模型迁移效果近乎为零。提出"怀疑者防御"策略可将谄媚降至5%，并建议将安全导向人格叠加在用户人格之下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态AI承诺通过人格提示（如"有创意"、"细致"）实现行为适应，以尊重用户多样化的价值观和沟通风格。但模型在多大程度上可以定制化而不破坏其对齐性（安全性、诚实性等）尚不明确，因此需要系统研究对齐与定制化之间的权衡关系。

Method: 在两种不同对齐强度的模型（Claude Sonnet强对齐、Nova Lite弱对齐）上，设置七种人格条件（包括基线、宜人性、外向性、开放性、怀疑者等），跨五项任务进行共1,800次运行实验，测量各条件下的谄媚行为（sycophancy）比例。

Result: 1) 强对齐模型上所有人格条件谄媚率均稳定在~15%（"对齐地板"）；2) 弱对齐模型上人格提示将谄媚率从5%推高至50%；3) 外向性（+20pp）和开放性（+15pp）的危害大于宜人性；4) 怀疑者人格将弱对齐模型的谄媚率降至5%；5) 人格效果的跨模型迁移几乎为零（ρ=0.006）。

Conclusion: 提出"对齐地板"作为设计原则：在部署人格定制化前需先测量模型的对齐地板，并在用户面向的人格之下叠加安全导向人格（如怀疑者），以实现在不牺牲对齐性的前提下提供个性化服务。

Abstract: A key promise of pluralistic AI is behavioral adaptation: persona prompts like "be creative" or "be thorough" let systems respect diverse user values and communication styles. But how much customization can a model absorb before its alignment breaks? We present the first controlled study of the alignment-customization tradeoff, testing seven persona conditions across five tasks on two models with different alignment strengths (1,800 runs). We discover the alignment floor: on a strongly-aligned model (Claude Sonnet), persona prompts have zero effect on sycophancy -- all conditions produce ~15%, a stable platform on which rich personalization is safe. On a weakly-aligned model (Nova Lite), the same personas shift sycophancy from 5% to 50% -- the floor is absent and customization becomes a safety liability. Surprisingly, Agreeableness is not the worst offender; Extraversion (+20pp) and Openness (+15pp) cause greater degradation. The constructive finding is the Skeptic defense: a critical-thinking persona reduces sycophancy to 5% even on the weak model -- the single largest effect in the study. Cross-model transfer of persona effects is near-zero ($ρ= 0.006$), meaning alignment testing must be per-model. We propose the alignment floor as a design principle: measure it before deploying persona customization, and layer safety-oriented personas underneath user-facing ones to enable personalization without compromising alignment.

</details>


### [212] [Designing Augmented Reality for Preschoolers on the Move](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27386)
*Supriya Khadka,Sanchari Das*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 这篇论文指出当前AR系统难以适应3-8岁幼儿的动态行为，并提出一个名为AnchorPlay AR的隐私保护、音频优先的空间应用概念原型，通过分离移动与视觉追踪来提升安全性和可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有商业和教育AR系统假设用户行为可预测且静止，但3-8岁幼儿动作 erratic、身体活跃、移动频繁，现有系统难以应对这些挑战。

Method: 通过对近期关于幼儿在AR中身体活动与空间学习的文献进行分析，识别当前移动AR部署中的摩擦点，并提出了AnchorPlay AR概念原型——采用音频引导移动、视觉增强仅在静止时刻使用的隐私保护方案。

Result: 识别出四项主要问题：动态运动时相机追踪失败、屏幕分心导致的身体安全隐患、物理标记周围的空间拥挤、以及持续环境监控的隐私风险。AnchorPlay AR通过分离移动与视觉追踪来应对这些问题。

Conclusion: 对于不断移动的幼儿，音频优先、视觉在静止时增强的AR框架比传统视觉追踪方案更安全、更适用。

Abstract: Advancements in augmented reality (AR) technologies offer immense potential for mobile experiences. However, most commercial and educational AR systems assume a baseline of predictable user behavior and stationary interaction. Preschoolers and children in early childhood education, specifically ages 3 to 8, are naturally erratic, physically dynamic, and prone to rapid locomotion, making them the ultimate stress test for mobile spatial computing. Through a focused analysis of recent literature on physical activity and spatial learning in AR for preschoolers, this paper identifies points of friction in current mobile deployments. We highlight recurring failures in camera tracking during dynamic movement, physical safety hazards caused by screen-induced distraction, spatial crowding around physical markers, and the privacy risks of continuous environmental surveillance. To address these challenges, we propose AnchorPlay AR, a conceptual prototype for a privacy-preserving, audio-first spatial application. By explicitly separating locomotion from visual tracking, AnchorPlay AR uses audio cues to safely guide movement and reserves visual augmentation for stationary moments, offering a safer framework for preschoolers in constant motion.

### [213] [What Catches the Eye? A Conjoint Study of Infographic Design Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27554)
*Amit Kumar Das,Karanbir Pelia,Manav Nitesh Ukani,Klaus Mueller*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本文通过选择联合分析（N=65）研究了信息图设计因素（比较类型、颜色、图形类型）对读者偏好的影响，发现比较类型贡献了58.5%的偏好差异，图形类型占29.2%，颜色仅占12.3%且无实际效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去研究孤立考察信息图设计因素（如图表类型、颜色、基准线），缺乏对读者如何权衡多个因素的了解。

Method: 采用基于选择的联合分析（choice-based conjoint study），65名参与者在一份模拟报纸页面上成对比较关于失业率的信息图，每个信息图在比较类型（无/美国平均值/百分比刻度）、颜色（红色/蓝色）和图形类型（单图标/图标系列/柱状图）三个属性上变化。

Result: 比较类型驱动了58.5%的偏好变异，图形类型占29.2%，颜色占12.3%。读者偏好百分比刻度和基准比较，颜色无实际效果。

Conclusion: 联合分析是一种实用且未被充分利用的可视化偏好研究方法，但本研究受限于单一主题和狭窄配色方案，外部有效性有限。

Abstract: Infographic designers balance many choices at once: chart type, color, and whether to add a benchmark or a scale. Past work studies these factors one at a time, so we know little about how readers weigh them against each other. We address this gap with a choice-based conjoint study (N = 65) in which participants viewed pairs of infographics on a mock newspaper page about unemployment. Each infographic varied across three attributes: comparison type (none, US average, percentage scale), color (red, blue), and graphic type (single icon, icon series, bar chart). Comparison type drove most of the preference variation (58.5%), followed by graphic type (29.2%) and color (12.3%). Readers favored percentage scale markers and benchmark comparisons; color had no practical effect. The percentage scale level adds axis information rather than a benchmark, so the comparison type result mixes two distinct ideas. A single topic and a narrow palette also limit external validity. We argue that conjoint analysis is a practical and underused tool for studying visualization preferences across many design dimensions.

### [217] [EyeSpy: Inferring Eye Gaze via Side-Channel Attacks Against Foveated Rendering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27939)
*Paul Maynard,Harris Amjad,Camila Molinares,Bo Ji,Brendan David-John*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一种利用动态注视点渲染（DFR）导致的GPU负载差异作为侧信道，从VR设备中重建用户注视点位置的攻击方法，并提出了有效的防御机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在启用DFR的VR系统中，眼动追踪数据即使被权限保护，仍会因注视点区域与外围区域的GPU负载差异而产生侧信道泄露风险，现有保护手段不足。

Method: 攻击者扫描不可见的高成本物体（HCO）跨越用户视野，记录游戏引擎暴露的渲染性能指标（帧率/帧时间），通过HCO与注视点重叠引起的性能波动与HCO已知位置的相关性，推断注视点坐标。

Result: 在Meta Quest Pro、Varjo XR-4和桌面平台上，平均注视点预测误差为1.1-4.4度，与典型眼动追踪器精度相当，且攻击可泛化到不同硬件、游戏引擎和DFR管线。

Conclusion: 设计了基于监督和无监督检测器的防御机制，可在短时间窗口内可靠识别攻击（F1分数0.99）。

Abstract: While eye tracking provides valuable capabilities for virtual reality, such as gaze interaction and dynamic foveated rendering (DFR), eye-tracking data can inadvertently reveal sensitive user information if not properly protected. Current protections, such as adding permission prompts or gatekeeping gaze data, are insufficient on DFR-enabled systems because gaze data is used internally to drive DFR. When DFR is implemented, objects in the fovea (i.e., immediate gaze area) incur a higher GPU workload than those in the periphery. This gaze-contingent workload creates a novel side channel, which can be leveraged to reconstruct gaze positions. Specifically, we design a novel attack that sweeps imperceptible high-cost objects (HCOs) across the user's field of view and logs rendering performance metrics (e.g., frame rate or frame time) commonly exposed through standard game engines. Then, we correlate variation in these metrics (caused by HCO-foveal overlap) with the known HCOs' positions to infer gaze coordinates directly without using eye-tracking APIs. Our experimental results show that mean gaze prediction errors (1.1-4.4 degrees) across the Meta Quest Pro, Varjo XR-4, and desktop platforms are comparable to typical eye-tracker accuracy. We demonstrate that the attack generalizes across various hardware platforms, standard game engines, and foveated rendering pipelines. Finally, we design defense mechanisms based on supervised and unsupervised detectors that can flag the attack reliably (F1 of 0.99) over short time windows.

### [219] [SmartIterator: Visual Analytics Workflows for Supervising Unsupervised Data Grouping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28219)
*Gennady Andrienko,Natalia Andrienko*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: SmartIterator 是一种可视化分析方法，将参数扫描产生的完整分组结果序列作为一级分析对象，通过三个方法族（密度聚类、分区聚类、主题建模）的结构化六阶段工作流，结合 IteraScope 可视化界面，引导分析师系统探索和评估无监督学习结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无监督学习方法虽不依赖人工标注，但对分组结果的选择和评估本身不应也是无监督的；现有方法缺少系统、可操作的指导来探索参数空间并理解数据结构随参数的变化。

Method: 提出 SmartIterator 框架，为每个方法族设计六阶段工作流（质量度量和概览→过渡稳定性评估→成员置信度评价→内容与上下文检查→循环原型验证→知情决策），并通过 IteraScope 可视化系统实现，结合质量指标图、语义颜色编码、一维分组嵌入（含 Sankey 过渡流和小提琴图）、二维分组嵌入（含 HDBSCAN 检测的循环原型）以及领域特定链接视图。

Result: 在三个数据集上验证：VAST Challenge 2011 模拟社交媒体消息（密度聚类，有真实标签验证）、EU 人口统计数据（约1500个 NUTS-3 区域，分区聚类）、30年 IEEE VIS 论文（NMF 主题建模）。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了可操作、方法特定的指导来导航参数空间，研究数据结构随配置变化的方式，并在领域上下文中建立分析理解，从而获得任何单一"最佳"结果都无法提供的关于数据的知识。

Abstract: Unsupervised learning methods -- topic modeling, partition-based and density-based clustering -- produce data groupings without human guidance, yet choosing and evaluating those groupings should not itself be unsupervised. We present \emph{SmartIterator}~(SI), a visual analytics approach that treats the full sequence of grouping results across a parameter sweep as a first-class analytical object. For each method family, SI provides a structured six-phase workflow that guides the analyst through systematic exploration of grouping results -- from quality-metric overview through transition-stability assessment, membership-confidence evaluation, content and context inspection, and recurrent-archetype verification to an informed decision -- building cumulative understanding of data structure along the way. The workflows are operationalized through \emph{IteraScope}~(IS), a coordinated visual display combining quality-metric charts with semantic color encoding, a 1D group embedding with Sankey-style transition flows and violin plots of membership confidence, a 2D group embedding with HDBSCAN-detected recurrent archetypes that highlights iterations capturing all persistent patterns, and domain-specific linked views for contextualized interpretation. We demonstrate the three workflows on: (1)~simulated social-media messages from the VAST Challenge 2011 (density-based clustering, validated against ground truth), (2)~EU population statistics across ${\sim}1\,500$ NUTS-3 regions (partition-based clustering), and (3)~30 years of IEEE VIS papers (NMF topic modeling). The workflows constitute the main contribution: they provide actionable, method-specific guidance for navigating parameter spaces, studying how data structure evolves across configurations, and grounding analytical understanding in domain context -- yielding knowledge about the data that no single ``best'' result can provide.

### [220] [The Decision to Verify: How Warmth and User Characteristics Shape Reliance on Conversational Agents for Information Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28498)
*Mert Yazan,Frederik Bungaran Ishak Situmeang,Suzan Verberne*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了混合交互范式（对话AI+网页搜索）是否能减少用户对AI的过度依赖。实验发现，尽管用户可以同时使用对话AI和网页搜索，过度依赖依然存在。用户是否进行事实核查主要取决于其既有认知（如对AI的信任倾向），而非答案本身的质量。温暖对话风格会间接增加对错误答案的认同，而使用额外AI源有助于提高准确性，传统网页搜索则不能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对话AI虽然便捷高效，但容易导致用户盲目信任而不进行事实核查，产生过度依赖问题。随着信息搜索向"对话AI+网页搜索"的混合交互范式发展，这种模式是否能够有效减少用户对AI的过度依赖，以及影响用户验证行为的深层因素是什么，是本研究要回答的核心问题。

Method: 采用混合被试问答实验设计，参与者与温暖型或中性型聊天机器人进行交互，同时可访问对话AI和网页搜索结果。通过实验数据考察用户对AI答案的依赖程度和事实核查行为。

Result: (1) 即使用户同时拥有对话和网页搜索渠道，过度依赖仍然存在；(2) 用户是否进行事实核查主要取决于其既有认知（如对聊天机器人的先验信任），而非答案本身特性，部分用户无论情境如何都会核查，部分则默认信任；(3) 温暖对话风格通过增加对错误答案的认同间接影响过度依赖；(4) 咨询额外AI源能预测更高准确性，而传统网页搜索则不能。

Conclusion: 本研究扩展了过度依赖研究：(a) 证明即使有事实核查渠道，过度依赖仍然存在；(b) 识别出验证行为是用户依赖型的；(c) 揭示了对话温暖风格对过度依赖的间接影响，为设计可信赖的对话式搜索系统提供了启示。

Abstract: Conversational artificial intelligence (AI) provides an efficient and convenient gateway to information access. However, it can cause overreliance when users blindly trust AI and accept its answers without fact-checking. Information search increasingly follows a hybrid interaction paradigm that combines conversational AI with web search, making fact-checking easier. In this paper, we examine whether this interaction paradigm is effective in curbing reliance. We further investigate the underlying factors (e.g., digital literacy and conversation warmth) that drive users to verify AI answers. We conduct a mixed-subjects question-answering experiment where participants interact with either a warm or a neutral chatbot. Our findings reveal that reliance persists despite users having access to both conversational and web search. The decision to verify is driven primarily by existing user perceptions (e.g., prior trust in chatbots) rather than answer properties, with some users fact-checking regardless of the context and others trusting chatbots by default. Warm conversational style has an indirect yet critical influence on reliance by increasing agreement with the chatbot when it is incorrect. Consulting additional AI sources predicts higher accuracy, while traditional web search does not. Our study extends overreliance research by: (a) demonstrating its persistence despite access to fact-checking, (b) identifying verification behavior as user-dependent, and (c) revealing conversational warmth's indirect effect on overreliance with implications for designing trustworthy conversational search systems.

### [221] [Not All Uncertainty Is Equal: How Uncertainty Granularity Shapes Human Verification in LLM-Assisted Decision Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28571)
*Mauricio Villavicencio,Sitong Pan,Qianwen Wang*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 研究表明，LLM输出中的不确定性粒度（输出级、关系级和词元级）显著影响用户决策行为。词元级不确定性增加用户对AI的认同，而输出级和关系级降低用户自信，关系级还会减少用户的外部验证行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将LLM的不确定性表达简化为单一数值或简单自然语言，忽略了LLM单次输出包含多个声明和推理步骤、每个步骤具有不同不确定性水平这一关键特性。

Method: 开展大规模被试间实验（N=192），让参与者在三种不同不确定性粒度（输出级、关系级、词元级）条件下使用LLM回答医学问题。

Result: 词元级不确定性增加用户与AI的认同；输出级和关系级不确定性降低用户对自身答案的自信；关系级不确定性减少用户的外部验证行为（如互联网搜索、检查URL），促使用户更依赖LLM及其不确定性提示。

Conclusion: 不确定性粒度显著影响用户与LLM输出的交互和验证方式，为构建鼓励适当质疑和验证行为的负责任LLM应用提供了具体设计指导。

Abstract: Despite warnings that LLMs can make mistakes, users often develop inappropriate trust and accept incorrect answers without critical evaluation. Uncertainty quantification (UQ), displaying LLMs' confidence, has emerged as a promising approach to calibrate user trust. However, prior empirical studies on uncertainty communication have treated uncertainty as a single numerical score or simple natural language expression. This simplification fails to capture a key property of LLM outputs: a single response often comprises multiple claims and reasoning steps, each with distinct levels of uncertainty. To address this gap, this study investigates uncertainty granularity (i.e., the extent to which uncertainty is expressed at different levels within an LLM response) and examines its impact on LLM-assisted decision-making. We conducted a large-scale, between-subjects study (N=192) in which participants answered medical questions using LLMs that displayed uncertainty at three different granularities: output-level (entire response), relation-level (individual reasoning steps), and token-level (specific words). Our findings reveal distinct behavioral effects as a function of uncertainty granularity. Token-level uncertainty increased users' agreement with the AI, whereas output- and relation-level uncertainty did not increase agreement but instead reduced users' confidence in their own answers. Notably, relation-level uncertainty also reduced external verification (i.e., internet searches, checking provided URLs), steering users away from independent fact-checking and toward reliance on the LLM and its accompanying uncertainty cues. Our findings demonstrate that uncertainty granularity significantly shapes how users interact with and verify LLM outputs, providing concrete design guidance for building responsible LLM applications that encourage appropriate skepticism and verification behaviors.

</details>


### [222] [AI in the Workplace: The Impact of AI on Perceived Job Decency and Meaningfulness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28680)
*Kuntal Ghosh,Marc Hassenzahl,Shadan Sadeghian*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本研究通过对24名来自IT、服务和医疗行业的员工访谈，探讨了AI对工作满意度的影响，发现AI对不同职业群体的工作体面性和意义感的影响存在差异，进而导致对整体工作满意度的预期变化各不相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注人机协作的工作绩效，而对员工体验（如工作满意度、工作体面性和意义感）的影响了解不足。

Method: 对24名来自IT、服务和医疗行业的员工进行半结构化访谈，分析他们对AI当前及未来对工作体面性和意义感影响的感知。

Result: AI对工作满意度的影响因职业领域而异：IT和医疗行业预期在工时等体面性方面满意度提升，但在社会形象等意义感方面下降；服务行业工时不改善，但社会地位因与AI工作而提升。

Conclusion: AI对员工体验的影响是复杂且分化的，需要针对不同职业领域采取差异化的人机协作设计策略。

Abstract: The proliferation of Artificial Intelligence (AI) in workplaces is transforming how we work. While existing research on human-AI collaboration at work often prioritizes performance, less is known about their experiential outcomes. Through interviews with 24 employees across Information Technology (IT), service-based, and healthcare sectors, this paper examines AI's impact on job satisfaction via perceptions of job decency and meaningfulness, now and in the future. Our results reveal that the anticipated impact of AI on overall job satisfaction varies with the occupational domain, with differing perceptions of its underlying decency and meaningfulness. For instance, IT and healthcare anticipate increased satisfaction with decency aspects like working hours but decreased satisfaction with meaningfulness aspects like social image due to misconceptions about AI handling most of their tasks. Conversely, service workers foresee no improvement in their working hours but a higher social standing due to the perceived status boost associated with working with AI.

</details>
